# 5000句职场英语双语完整版 (5000 Bilingual Business Sentences)

> **老板专属完整版**：修复了语法结构，配齐了**中英双语对照**！直接全覆盖日常交流。每天翻一翻，语感自然来。

**1.** This would be mutually beneficial for the client presentation before the holidays.
   *这对...是互利的：客户演示（节假日前）。*

**2.** I'm planning to finalize the cybersecurity protocols by tomorrow morning.
   *我打算敲定网络安全协议（明早前）。*

**3.** There seems to be a misunderstanding about the terms of service update before the end of the day.
   *在...上似乎有误解：服务条款更新（今天下班前）。*

**4.** I think we have a deal on the user interface improvements by the end of the month.
   *我想我们在...上达成一致了：用户界面改进（月底前）。*

**5.** This would be mutually beneficial for the customer support tickets by next week.
   *这对...是互利的：客户支持工单（下周前）。*

**6.** One area for improvement is the sales pipeline by tomorrow morning.
   *一个需要改进的地方是销售漏斗（明早前）。*

**7.** We might need extra hands for the strategic planning session before the holidays.
   *我们在...上可能需要额外人手：战略规划会议（节假日前）。*

**8.** One area for improvement is the office relocation at your earliest convenience.
   *一个需要改进的地方是办公室搬迁（在您方便的时候尽早）。*

**9.** Just following up on the emergency response plan by tomorrow morning.
   *跟进一下应急响应计划（明早前）。*

**10.** I really appreciate your help with the sales pipeline before the end of the day.
   *非常感谢你帮忙处理销售漏斗（今天下班前）。*

**11.** Can you give me an update on the customer retention plan before the holidays.
   *你能给我更新一下...的情况吗：客户留存计划（节假日前）。*

**12.** Just following up on the data privacy regulations at your earliest convenience.
   *跟进一下数据隐私法规（在您方便的时候尽早）。*

**13.** Would you be open to grabbing a coffee to discuss the offshore development team by tomorrow morning.
   *你愿意喝杯咖啡讨论一下...吗：离岸开发团队（明早前）。*

**14.** As far as I know, they approved the updated timeline at your earliest convenience.
   *据我所知，他们已经批准了更新后的时间表（在您方便的时候尽早）。*

**15.** So what you're saying is we should cancel the investor pitch deck by next week.
   *所以你的意思是我们应该取消投资人商业计划书（下周前）。*

**16.** I'm planning to finalize the quarterly review at your earliest convenience.
   *我打算敲定季度评估（在您方便的时候尽早）。*

**17.** I'm afraid that's non-negotiable regarding the mobile app development by next week.
   *恐怕在...上没得商量：移动应用开发（下周前）。*

**18.** We need to schedule a meeting for the software upgrade before the holidays.
   *我们需要为...安排一个会议：软件升级（节假日前）。*

**19.** I have a few questions regarding the feedback from the beta test by tomorrow morning.
   *关于...我有些问题：Beta测试反馈（明早前）。*

**20.** Let's stay in touch regarding the cross-functional collaboration by the end of the month.
   *让我们就...保持联系：跨部门协作（月底前）。*

**21.** I was wondering if we could discuss the new marketing strategy as soon as possible.
   *不知我们能否讨论一下新营销战略（尽快）。*

**22.** Is there any flexibility on the tax return preparation by tomorrow morning.
   *在...方面有弹性吗：报税准备（明早前）。*

**23.** I completely agree with the plan for the vendor selection before the end of the day.
   *我完全同意关于...的计划：供应商选择（今天下班前）。*

**24.** We need this finalized for the training materials by the end of the month.
   *我们需要为...敲定此事：培训材料（月底前）。*

**25.** I'm writing to inform you about the intellectual property filing before the holidays.
   *我写信是为了通知你关于知识产权备案（节假日前）。*

**26.** What if we delay the customer support tickets in the upcoming meeting.
   *如果我们推迟...会怎样：客户支持工单（在接下来的会议上）。*

**27.** Does this time work for discussing the emergency response plan next quarter.
   *这个时间方便讨论...吗：应急响应计划（下季度）。*

**28.** We need to schedule a meeting for the internal audit before the end of the day.
   *我们需要为...安排一个会议：内部审计（今天下班前）。*

**29.** There's a slight delay with the disaster recovery plan by the end of the month.
   *在...上有轻微的延误：灾难恢复计划（月底前）。*

**30.** Just following up on the internal audit next quarter.
   *跟进一下内部审计（下季度）。*

**31.** How can we align our goals on the investor pitch deck in the upcoming meeting.
   *我们如何能在...上达成目标一致：投资人商业计划书（在接下来的会议上）。*

**32.** I think we have a deal on the pricing strategy adjustment in the upcoming meeting.
   *我想我们在...上达成一致了：定价策略调整（在接下来的会议上）。*

**33.** Just following up on the end-of-year bonuses before the holidays.
   *跟进一下年终奖金（节假日前）。*

**34.** Just following up on the social media campaign in the upcoming meeting.
   *跟进一下社交媒体推广（在接下来的会议上）。*

**35.** I will be out of office, please handle the customer support tickets by the end of the month.
   *我将休假，请处理客户支持工单（月底前）。*

**36.** Could you take the lead on the design mockups during the next sprint.
   *你能否牵头负责设计稿（在下个冲刺阶段）。*

**37.** Please find attached the document for the disaster recovery plan next quarter.
   *请查收附件中关于...的文档：灾难恢复计划（下季度）。*

**38.** Please find attached the document for the internal audit before the holidays.
   *请查收附件中关于...的文档：内部审计（节假日前）。*

**39.** I completely agree with the plan for the Q3 financial report during the next sprint.
   *我完全同意关于...的计划：Q3财报（在下个冲刺阶段）。*

**40.** I completely agree with the plan for the competitive analysis by next week.
   *我完全同意关于...的计划：竞品分析（下周前）。*

**41.** I'm writing to inform you about the client presentation before the end of the day.
   *我写信是为了通知你关于客户演示（今天下班前）。*

**42.** I was wondering if we could discuss the marketing ROI by the end of the month.
   *不知我们能否讨论一下营销投资回报率（月底前）。*

**43.** As far as I know, they approved the investor pitch deck at your earliest convenience.
   *据我所知，他们已经批准了投资人商业计划书（在您方便的时候尽早）。*

**44.** It looks like we have an issue with the sales targets for this month during the next sprint.
   *看来我们在...遇到了问题：本月销售目标（在下个冲刺阶段）。*

**45.** Moving on to the SEO optimization strategy by the end of the month.
   *接下来我们进入SEO优化策略（月底前）。*

**46.** It looks like we have an issue with the Q3 financial report during the next sprint.
   *看来我们在...遇到了问题：Q3财报（在下个冲刺阶段）。*

**47.** Let me double-check the details of the customer retention plan at your earliest convenience.
   *让我再核实一下...的细节：客户留存计划（在您方便的时候尽早）。*

**48.** How are we doing with the key performance indicators before the end of the day.
   *我们...进展如何了：关键绩效指标(KPI)（今天下班前）。*

**49.** I understand your concern about the quarterly review during the next sprint.
   *我理解你对...的担忧：季度评估（在下个冲刺阶段）。*

**50.** We need to schedule a meeting for the user acquisition cost at your earliest convenience.
   *我们需要为...安排一个会议：用户获取成本（在您方便的时候尽早）。*

**51.** Could you take the lead on the end-of-year bonuses in the upcoming meeting.
   *你能否牵头负责年终奖金（在接下来的会议上）。*

**52.** Is there any flexibility on the offshore development team by the end of the month.
   *在...方面有弹性吗：离岸开发团队（月底前）。*

**53.** To help me prioritize, should I focus on the strategic planning session before the holidays.
   *为了帮我排期，我是否应该专注于战略规划会议（节假日前）。*

**54.** Why don't we review the cybersecurity protocols before the end of the day.
   *我们为什么不回顾一下网络安全协议（今天下班前）。*

**55.** Make sure to update the updated timeline by tomorrow morning.
   *务必更新更新后的时间表（明早前）。*

**56.** This would be mutually beneficial for the intellectual property filing by tomorrow morning.
   *这对...是互利的：知识产权备案（明早前）。*

**57.** Great job on the team restructuring as soon as possible.
   *在...上做得很好：团队重组（尽快）。*

**58.** So what you're saying is we should cancel the emergency response plan during the next sprint.
   *所以你的意思是我们应该取消应急响应计划（在下个冲刺阶段）。*

**59.** I understand your concern about the Q3 financial report before the end of the day.
   *我理解你对...的担忧：Q3财报（今天下班前）。*

**60.** What if we delay the inventory management system by next week.
   *如果我们推迟...会怎样：库存管理系统（下周前）。*

**61.** Please let me know your availability for the team restructuring during the next sprint.
   *请告诉我你什么时候有空处理团队重组（在下个冲刺阶段）。*

**62.** How can we align our goals on the backend API integration at your earliest convenience.
   *我们如何能在...上达成目标一致：后端API集成（在您方便的时候尽早）。*

**63.** What could we improve for the annual company retreat before the holidays.
   *为了...我们能改进什么：公司年会（节假日前）。*

**64.** Just following up on the risk assessment document by the end of the month.
   *跟进一下风险评估文件（月底前）。*

**65.** Just following up on the hiring process at your earliest convenience.
   *跟进一下招聘流程（在您方便的时候尽早）。*

**66.** How are we doing with the cloud storage costs before the end of the day.
   *我们...进展如何了：云存储成本（今天下班前）。*

**67.** I was wondering if we could discuss the remote work policy before the end of the day.
   *不知我们能否讨论一下远程办公政策（今天下班前）。*

**68.** I have a few questions regarding the competitive analysis by the end of the month.
   *关于...我有些问题：竞品分析（月底前）。*

**69.** I will be out of office, please handle the office relocation before the end of the day.
   *我将休假，请处理办公室搬迁（今天下班前）。*

**70.** Sorry to interrupt, but we need to talk about the performance metrics during the next sprint.
   *抱歉打断一下，但我们需要谈谈绩效指标（在下个冲刺阶段）。*

**71.** Sorry to interrupt, but we need to talk about the financial forecasting before the holidays.
   *抱歉打断一下，但我们需要谈谈财务预测（节假日前）。*

**72.** Could you take the lead on the team restructuring before the end of the day.
   *你能否牵头负责团队重组（今天下班前）。*

**73.** Let's brainstorm some ideas for the annual company retreat by next week.
   *让我们为...头脑风暴一下：公司年会（下周前）。*

**74.** Can we get a quick alignment on the internal audit in the upcoming meeting.
   *我们能快速对齐一下...吗：内部审计（在接下来的会议上）。*

**75.** Could you please send me the competitive analysis at your earliest convenience.
   *请发给我竞品分析（在您方便的时候尽早）。*

**76.** Can we get a quick alignment on the hiring process next quarter.
   *我们能快速对齐一下...吗：招聘流程（下季度）。*

**77.** Can we get a quick alignment on the executive summary by next week.
   *我们能快速对齐一下...吗：执行摘要（下周前）。*

**78.** What could we improve for the sales targets for this month by next week.
   *为了...我们能改进什么：本月销售目标（下周前）。*

**79.** Unfortunately, we won't be able to proceed with the emergency response plan as soon as possible.
   *很遗憾，我们无法继续推进应急响应计划（尽快）。*

**80.** I think we have a deal on the server migration project by tomorrow morning.
   *我想我们在...上达成一致了：服务器迁移项目（明早前）。*

**81.** I'm planning to finalize the office relocation by tomorrow morning.
   *我打算敲定办公室搬迁（明早前）。*

**82.** It looks like we have an issue with the user interface improvements at your earliest convenience.
   *看来我们在...遇到了问题：用户界面改进（在您方便的时候尽早）。*

**83.** Let's stay in touch regarding the competitive analysis by the end of the month.
   *让我们就...保持联系：竞品分析（月底前）。*

**84.** I really appreciate your help with the training materials by the end of the month.
   *非常感谢你帮忙处理培训材料（月底前）。*

**85.** How can we align our goals on the sales pipeline during the next sprint.
   *我们如何能在...上达成目标一致：销售漏斗（在下个冲刺阶段）。*

**86.** I have a few questions regarding the mobile app development next quarter.
   *关于...我有些问题：移动应用开发（下季度）。*

**87.** I appreciate the feedback on the terms of service update by the end of the month.
   *感谢你对...的反馈：服务条款更新（月底前）。*

**88.** Why don't we review the new feature rollout by the end of the month.
   *我们为什么不回顾一下新功能发布（月底前）。*

**89.** To help me prioritize, should I focus on the updated timeline before the holidays.
   *为了帮我排期，我是否应该专注于更新后的时间表（节假日前）。*

**90.** Please find attached the document for the design mockups by tomorrow morning.
   *请查收附件中关于...的文档：设计稿（明早前）。*

**91.** Can we get a quick alignment on the intellectual property filing before the end of the day.
   *我们能快速对齐一下...吗：知识产权备案（今天下班前）。*

**92.** Sorry to interrupt, but we need to talk about the key performance indicators by the end of the month.
   *抱歉打断一下，但我们需要谈谈关键绩效指标(KPI)（月底前）。*

**93.** Make sure to update the QA testing results by the end of the month.
   *务必更新QA测试结果（月底前）。*

**94.** There seems to be a misunderstanding about the financial forecasting by tomorrow morning.
   *在...上似乎有误解：财务预测（明早前）。*

   *我将休假，请处理后端API集成（节假日前）。*

**100.** What could we improve for the customer retention plan as soon as possible.
   *为了...我们能改进什么：客户留存计划（尽快）。*
